        </div>

    </div>
    {{/deferred}}
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            window.onerror = function (msg, url, line, col, error) {
                try {
                    var extra = !col ? '' : '\ncolumn: ' + col;
                    extra += !error ? '' : '\nerror: ' + error;
                    var stack = null;
                    if (error && error.stack)
                        stack = error.stack.toString();
                    var message = "Error: " + msg + "\nurl: " + url + "\nline: " + line + extra + '\nstacktrace: ' + stack + '\nlocation: ' + window.location.href;

                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: 'error/logJsError',
                        data: { message: message },
                        async: true
                    });
                } finally {
                    //setTimeout(function () { window.location.href = 'jsError.html'; }, 200);
                }

                window.__logCustomJsWarning = function (msg) {
                    try {
                        var message = 'Warning: ' + msg + '\nlocation: ' + window.location.href;

                        $.ajax({
                            type: 'POST',
                            url: 'error/logJsWarning',
                            data: { message: message },
                            async: true
                        });
                    } catch (e) { }
                };
            };

            (function () {
                var __BASE_TITLE__ = document.title;
                window.__updateTitle = function (title) {
                    var newTitle = title ? title + ' - ' + __BASE_TITLE__ : __BASE_TITLE__;
                    var userForWatchLogin = window.sessionStorage.getItem('userForWatchMail');
                    if (userForWatchLogin) {
                        newTitle = '🔎 ' + userForWatchLogin + '; ' + newTitle;
                    }
                    document.title = newTitle;
                }
            })();
        </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            $(function () {
                $(document.documentElement).addClass("i-bem").attr("onclick", "return {'page': {}}");

            showKdTelecom: false,
                };
        </script>
